UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_13 = min(max(u_xlat16_13, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);

    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_24.yyy;
    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat16_24.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);

    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;

#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;

    u_xlat16_35 = max(u_xlat16_35, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * 6.0;

    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_37 = exp2(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;

    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_38 = min(max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.zzz * _SHBotColor.xyz;

    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xzw * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_35) + 1.03999996;

    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_38 * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_9.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_37 = min(max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_7.y + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_39 / u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz;

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_35) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;

    u_xlat16_2.xyw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat16_24.xxx + u_xlat16_2.xyw;

#endif

    u_xlat16_37 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);

    u_xlat16_24.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_24.x + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;

    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

mediump float u_xlat16_70;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat59 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat59 = max(u_xlat59, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat59 = inversesqrt(u_xlat59);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat59) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * u_xlat19.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_58 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_58 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_58);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_58) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat3.xy,u_xlat3.z);
    u_xlat3.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat5.xy,u_xlat5.z);
    u_xlat3.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat5.xy,u_xlat5.z);
    u_xlat3.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat5.xy,u_xlat5.z);
    u_xlat3.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_58 = dot(u_xlat3, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_58 = u_xlat16_58 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_4.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb59 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb59 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb3 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb3 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb59 = u_xlatb59 || u_xlatb3;
    u_xlat16_58 = (u_xlatb59) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_58;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat59 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat59 = max(u_xlat59, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat59 = inversesqrt(u_xlat59);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat59) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat59) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_61 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_61 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_61);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_61) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_61 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_61 = min(max(u_xlat16_61, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_61 = clamp(u_xlat16_61, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_63 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_63 = min(max(u_xlat16_63, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_63 = clamp(u_xlat16_63, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_7 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_7.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_25 = min(max(u_xlat16_25, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_25 = clamp(u_xlat16_25, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_7.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_44 = max(u_xlat16_44, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_44 = min(u_xlat16_44, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_44 * u_xlat16_44;
    u_xlat16_27 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_7.z));
    u_xlat16_27 = u_xlat16_27 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_27 = exp2(u_xlat16_27);
    u_xlat16_27 = min(u_xlat16_27, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_7.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_46 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_65 = (-u_xlat16_25) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_65);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * u_xlat16_10.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat60 = u_xlat16_1.y * u_xlat16_1.y;
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat16_1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat26 = u_xlat60 * 0.125 + u_xlat7;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat26 + 0.125;
    u_xlat60 = u_xlat60 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat7);
    u_xlat11.y = u_xlat60 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_12.xy = max(u_xlat11.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_12.xy = u_xlat16_12.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_31.xyz = u_xlat16_12.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_31.xyz;
    u_xlat16_65 = dot((-u_xlat3.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_65 = u_xlat16_65 + u_xlat16_65;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_65)) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_65 = (-u_xlat16_61) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_66 = u_xlat16_65 * u_xlat16_65;

    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_13 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_13;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb11 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb11 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb11 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_13 = min(max(u_xlat16_13, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_13 = clamp(u_xlat16_13, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_24.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_24.yyy;
    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat16_24.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyw;
    u_xlat16_24.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_24.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_24.x);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_24.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_24.x = dot((-u_xlat11.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_24.x = u_xlat16_24.x + u_xlat16_24.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-u_xlat16_24.xxx) + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_24.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_24.x = min(max(u_xlat16_24.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_24.x = clamp(u_xlat16_24.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_35 = max(u_xlat16_35, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_35) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_37 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = log2(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_37 = exp2(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_38 = min(max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_38 = clamp(u_xlat16_38, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_37 = exp2(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_39) * vec2(u_xlat16_39) + vec2(1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xxx;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_4.y * u_xlat16_4.y;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat16_4.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat11.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat22 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_7.xz = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_7.xz = u_xlat16_7.xz * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.zzz * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_7.xzw;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xzw * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_35) + 1.03999996;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_38 * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_9.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) + (-u_xlat16_9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_24.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_24.x = log2(u_xlat16_24.x);
    u_xlat16_24.x = u_xlat16_24.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat16_24.x = exp2(u_xlat16_24.x);
    u_xlat16_24.x = (-u_xlat16_24.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xzw;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_37 = min(max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_7.y + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_39 / u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_35) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = min(u_xlat16_7.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyw * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyw * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyw * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat16_24.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_24.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlatb0 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_24.x = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_24.x = (u_xlatb0) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_24.x;
    u_xlat16_24.x = u_xlat16_24.x + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_37 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_24.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_24.x + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.x = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat10_0.x + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat16_24.x = (-u_xlat16_24.x) + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_24.x = clamp(u_xlat16_24.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_24.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyw + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;

float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];

    return;

    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_20.x * u_xlat16_1.x + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat16_20.x = u_xlat10_57 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_1.x) + u_xlat16_20.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_20.x = log2(u_xlat16_61);
    u_xlat16_20.x = u_xlat16_20.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat16_20.x = exp2(u_xlat16_20.x);
    u_xlat16_20.x = (-u_xlat16_20.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_20.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_20.xyz = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat16_20.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_20.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_5.w;
    return;
}

mediump float u_xlat16_38;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.yyy;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot((-u_xlat11.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_36)) + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);

    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_37) + 1.03999996;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_6.x * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.w;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) + (-u_xlat16_9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = log2(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat16_36 = exp2(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;

    u_xlat16_38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_38);

    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_14;
    u_xlat16_14 = min(u_xlat16_14, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_14) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = min(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _SHshadow + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlatb0 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_36 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = (u_xlatb0) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_37 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_36 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.x = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat10_0.x + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_18;
float u_xlat22;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.yyy;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot((-u_xlat11.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_36)) + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_37 = max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_37) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_38 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_38 = exp2(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_38 = min(u_xlat16_38, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_28.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_17) * vec2(u_xlat16_17) + vec2(1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_28.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_28.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_28.xxx;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat11.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat22 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = u_xlat16_7.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_37) + 1.03999996;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_6.x * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) + (-u_xlat16_9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = log2(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat16_36 = exp2(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _SHshadow + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlatb0 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_36 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = (u_xlatb0) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_37 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_36 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.x = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat10_0.x + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    return;
}

	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _viweoffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SHshadow;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _RimLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMapMul;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SunShiftOffuse2;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _glossiness_1Y;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _specularColor2;

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(7) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatTex;
in mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
bool u_xlatb11;
mediump float u_xlat16_13;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
float u_xlat22;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_24;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_13 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_13;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb11 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb11 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb11 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_13 = min(max(u_xlat16_13, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_13 = clamp(u_xlat16_13, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_24.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_24.yyy;
    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat16_24.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyw;
    u_xlat16_24.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_24.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_24.x);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_24.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_24.x = dot((-u_xlat11.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_24.x = u_xlat16_24.x + u_xlat16_24.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-u_xlat16_24.xxx) + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_24.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_24.x = min(max(u_xlat16_24.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_24.x = clamp(u_xlat16_24.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_35 = max(u_xlat16_35, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_35) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_37 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = log2(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_37 = exp2(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_38 = min(max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_38 = clamp(u_xlat16_38, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_37 = exp2(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_39) * vec2(u_xlat16_39) + vec2(1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xxx;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_4.y * u_xlat16_4.y;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat16_4.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat11.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat22 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_7.xz = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_7.xz = u_xlat16_7.xz * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.zzz * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_7.xzw;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.zzz * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_7.xzw;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xzw * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_35) + 1.03999996;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_38 * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.w;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_9.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) + (-u_xlat16_9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_24.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xzw;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_7.y + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_39 / u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_35) * u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = min(u_xlat16_5.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_13) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_24.x * u_xlat16_24.x;
    u_xlat16_24.x = log2(u_xlat16_24.x);
    u_xlat16_24.x = u_xlat16_24.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat16_24.x = exp2(u_xlat16_24.x);
    u_xlat16_24.x = (-u_xlat16_24.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat16_13, 0.959999979);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _MatTex_ST.x + _MatTex_ST.z;
    u_xlat0.y = 0.0;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_MatTex, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat16_2.xyw * _RampTexColor.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat16_24.xxx + u_xlat16_2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_24.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlatb0 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_24.x = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_24.x = (u_xlatb0) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_24.x;
    u_xlat16_24.x = u_xlat16_24.x + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_37 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_24.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_24.x + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.x = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat10_0.x + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat16_24.x = (-u_xlat16_24.x) + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_24.x = clamp(u_xlat16_24.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_24.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyw + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;

out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);

{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat59 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat59 = max(u_xlat59, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat59 = inversesqrt(u_xlat59);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat59) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * u_xlat19.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;

    u_xlat16_58 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_58);

    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;

    u_xlat59 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat3.xy).x;
    u_xlatb59 = u_xlat59<u_xlat3.z;
    u_xlat3.x = (u_xlatb59) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    u_xlat59 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat5.xy).x;

    u_xlat16_8.xzw = max(u_xlat16_8.xzw, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_8.xzw = min(u_xlat16_8.xzw, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xzw * vec3(u_xlat16_27) + u_xlat16_6.xyw;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = max(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = min(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_27) + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_58 = min(_AdditionalLightsCount.x, unity_LightData.y);
    u_xlati0 = int(u_xlat16_58);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    for(int u_xlati_loop_1 = 0 ; u_xlati_loop_1<u_xlati0 ; u_xlati_loop_1++)
    {
        u_xlat38 = float(u_xlati_loop_1);
        u_xlatb57 = u_xlat38<2.0;
        u_xlat16_8.xy = (bool(u_xlatb57)) ? unity_LightIndices[0].xy : unity_LightIndices[0].zw;
        u_xlat2.x = u_xlat38 + -2.0;
        u_xlat38 = (u_xlatb57) ? u_xlat38 : u_xlat2.x;
        u_xlatb38 = u_xlat38<1.0;
        u_xlat16_58 = (u_xlatb38) ? u_xlat16_8.x : u_xlat16_8.y;
        u_xlati38 = int(u_xlat16_58);
        u_xlat2.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz) + _AdditionalLightsPositionDynamicIndex(u_xlati38).xyz;
        u_xlat57 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
        u_xlat57 = max(u_xlat57, 6.10351563e-05);
        u_xlat59 = inversesqrt(u_xlat57);
        u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat59) * u_xlat2.xyz;
        u_xlat59 = float(1.0) / u_xlat57;
        u_xlat57 = u_xlat57 * _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati38).x + _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati38).y;
        u_xlat57 = clamp(u_xlat57, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat57 = u_xlat57 * u_xlat59;
        u_xlat16_58 = dot(_AdditionalLightsSpotDirDynamicIndex(u_xlati38).xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
        u_xlat16_58 = u_xlat16_58 * _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati38).z + _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati38).w;
        u_xlat16_58 = clamp(u_xlat16_58, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_58 = u_xlat16_58 * u_xlat16_58;
        u_xlat57 = u_xlat57 * u_xlat16_58;
        u_xlat16_58 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
        u_xlat16_58 = clamp(u_xlat16_58, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_58) * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
        u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _AdditionalLightsColorDynamicIndex(u_xlati38).xyz;
        u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(u_xlat57) + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    }
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlatb0 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_58 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_58 = (u_xlatb0) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_58;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.x = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(u_xlat16_4.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_58 = u_xlat16_58 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_58 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_58 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat10_0.x + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat16_58 = (-u_xlat16_58) + u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_58 = clamp(u_xlat16_58, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(u_xlat16_61);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat16_4.x = exp2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_23.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat16_4.xxx + u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_58) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_23.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_5.w;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;

    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

in mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
bool u_xlatb2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
bool u_xlatb3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;

vec2 u_xlat11;

uint u_xlatu19;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_20;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
bool u_xlatb21;
mediump float u_xlat16_25;
float u_xlat26;
mediump float u_xlat16_27;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_31;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_32;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_33;
float u_xlat38;
int u_xlati38;
bool u_xlatb38;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
mediump float u_xlat16_46;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_50;
mediump float u_xlat16_51;
float u_xlat57;
mediump float u_xlat16_57;
bool u_xlatb57;
mediump float u_xlat16_58;
float u_xlat59;
bool u_xlatb59;
float u_xlat60;
mediump float u_xlat16_61;
mediump float u_xlat16_63;
mediump float u_xlat16_65;
mediump float u_xlat16_66;
mediump float u_xlat16_67;
mediump float u_xlat16_69;
mediump float u_xlat16_70;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat19.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat59 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat59 = max(u_xlat59, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat59 = inversesqrt(u_xlat59);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat59) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * u_xlat19.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_58 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_58 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_58);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_58) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat3.xy,u_xlat3.z);
    u_xlat3.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat5.xy,u_xlat5.z);
    u_xlat3.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat5.xy,u_xlat5.z);
    u_xlat3.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat5.xy,u_xlat5.z);
    u_xlat3.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_58 = dot(u_xlat3, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_58 = u_xlat16_58 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_4.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb59 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb59 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb3 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb3 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb59 = u_xlatb59 || u_xlatb3;
    u_xlat16_58 = (u_xlatb59) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_58;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat59 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat59 = max(u_xlat59, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat59 = inversesqrt(u_xlat59);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat59) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat59) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_61 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_61 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_61);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_61) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_61 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_61 = min(max(u_xlat16_61, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_61 = clamp(u_xlat16_61, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_63 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
