UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatTex;
in mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_18;
float u_xlat22;
mediump float u_xlat16_25;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.yyy;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot((-u_xlat11.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_36)) + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_37 = max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_37) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_38 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_38 = exp2(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_38 = min(u_xlat16_38, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_28.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_17) * vec2(u_xlat16_17) + vec2(1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_28.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_28.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_28.xxx;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat11.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat22 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = u_xlat16_7.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_37) + 1.03999996;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_6.x * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = min(u_xlat16_6.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * 0.75 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14 = _SHshadow + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_14) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_25 = log2(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat16_25 = exp2(u_xlat16_25);
    u_xlat16_25 = (-u_xlat16_25) + 2.0;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat16_14, 0.959999979);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _MatTex_ST.x + _MatTex_ST.z;
    u_xlat0.y = 0.0;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_MatTex, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xyw * _RampTexColor.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_25) + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlatb0 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_25 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_25 = (u_xlatb0) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_25;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_37 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_25 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.x = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat10_0.x + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat16_25 = (-u_xlat16_25) + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_25 = clamp(u_xlat16_25, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * u_xlat16_3.xyw + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;

    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);

    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_DigiDistore);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;

UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatTex;
in mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_18;
float u_xlat22;
mediump float u_xlat16_25;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.yyy;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot((-u_xlat11.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 + u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_36)) + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_37 = max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_37) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_38 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_38 = exp2(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_38 = min(u_xlat16_38, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_28.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_17) * vec2(u_xlat16_17) + vec2(1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_28.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_28.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_28.xxx;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat22 = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat11.x);
    u_xlat0.y = u_xlat0.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat22 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = max(u_xlat0.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = u_xlat16_7.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_37) + 1.03999996;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_6.x * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) + (-u_xlat16_9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14 = _SHshadow + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_14) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_25 = log2(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat16_25 = exp2(u_xlat16_25);
    u_xlat16_25 = (-u_xlat16_25) + 2.0;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat16_14, 0.959999979);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * _MatTex_ST.x + _MatTex_ST.z;
    u_xlat0.y = 0.0;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_MatTex, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xyw * _RampTexColor.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyw * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyw * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyw * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_25) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlatb0 = _DigiBaseColor1.w<0.00999999978;
    u_xlat16_25 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_25 = (u_xlatb0) ? -1.0 : u_xlat16_25;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat16_37 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_25 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat10_0.x = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat10_0.x + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat16_25 = (-u_xlat16_25) + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_25 = clamp(u_xlat16_25, 0.0, 1.0);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * u_xlat16_3.xyw + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    return;
}

#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	vec4 _ScreenParams;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerDraw {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LODFade;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightIndices[2];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _OutlineColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OutlineWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Offset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _lightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _FarWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _NearWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _color1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _ScreenResolution;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _OutlineMap;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump float vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
float u_xlat9;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0 = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat9 = max(u_xlat9, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat9 = inversesqrt(u_xlat9);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat9) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat9 = inversesqrt(u_xlat9);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat9) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat9 = dot(_lightDir.xyz, _lightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat9 = inversesqrt(u_xlat9);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat9) * _lightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-_OutlineColor.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz + _OutlineColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = textureLod(_OutlineMap, in_TEXCOORD0.xy, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat1.w * abs(_Offset);
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat3.yy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1].xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0].xy * u_xlat3.xx + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2].xy * u_xlat3.zz + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat9 = dot(u_xlat3.xy, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat9 = inversesqrt(u_xlat9);
    u_xlat3.xy = vec2(u_xlat9) * u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy / _ScreenParams.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * _ScreenResolution.yy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat1.y * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1].w;
    u_xlat9 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0].w * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat9;
    u_xlat9 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2].w * u_xlat1.z + u_xlat9;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat9 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3].w;
    u_xlat0.yz = vec2(u_xlat9) * u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.150000006, 0.00462962966, 0.00462962966);
    u_xlat2.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].x;
    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].y;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat0.yz / u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat1.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].xyz * u_xlat1.zzz + u_xlat1.xyw;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat3.xy + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat3.xy, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat3.x = sqrt(u_xlat3.x);
    u_xlat3.x = max(u_xlat3.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat3.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 100.0;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat3.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz / abs(u_xlat3.zzz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].z;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].z;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].z;
    u_xlat1.w = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].z;
    u_xlat0.w = 1.0;
    gl_Position.z = dot(u_xlat1, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].x;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].x;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].x;
    gl_Position.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].y;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].y;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].y;
    gl_Position.y = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat0.yzw);
    u_xlat0.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].w;
    u_xlat0.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].w;
    gl_Position.w = dot(u_xlat0.xy, u_xlat0.zw);
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

precision highp float;

    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 _DigiST1;
uniform 	mediump float _DigiChange;
uniform 	float _DigiScale;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump float u_xlat16_1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
float u_xlat12;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = vec2(0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = max(u_xlat12, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = min(u_xlat16_1, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = (-u_xlat16_1) + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(0.0500000007, 0.0500000007, 0.0500000007);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_1) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(_DigiScale) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat2.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat2.zzz + u_xlat2.xyw;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat2.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.w = clamp(u_xlat0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0.x = in_TEXCOORD0.y * 2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat0.z = (-_DigiChange) * 2.0 + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.z = clamp(u_xlat0.z, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyw = in_TEXCOORD0.xyy;
    vs_TEXCOORD2 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat2.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat2.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat2.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_2 = (-_DigiBaseColor0) + _DigiBaseColor1;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1.xxxx * u_xlat16_2 + _DigiBaseColor0;
    u_xlat10_3.xy = texture2D(_ClothTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xy;
    u_xlatb9 = u_xlat16_1.w>=u_xlat10_3.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = (u_xlatb9) ? u_xlat0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat10_3.x * u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _DigiChange + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat10_3.y * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _DigiHighColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;

    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(_DigiScale) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyw * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = max(u_xlat12, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.w = min(max(u_xlat1.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.w = clamp(u_xlat1.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_COLOR0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat12 = in_TEXCOORD0.y * 2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat1.z = (-_DigiChange) * 2.0 + u_xlat12;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.z = min(max(u_xlat1.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.z = clamp(u_xlat1.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyw = in_TEXCOORD0.xyy;
    vs_TEXCOORD2 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#endif

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;

mediump float u_xlat16_10;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0 = vs_TEXCOORD1.w * vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _DigiChange;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = (-_DigiBaseColor0) + _DigiBaseColor1;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_1.xxxx * u_xlat16_2 + _DigiBaseColor0;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = texture(_ClothTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xy;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb9 = !!(u_xlat16_1.w>=u_xlat16_3.x);
#else
    u_xlatb9 = u_xlat16_1.w>=u_xlat16_3.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_10 = (u_xlatb9) ? u_xlat0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_10;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _DigiChange + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * _DigiHighColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_10) * u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;

    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
